Trace-FOSS - OpenAPI Documentation

Trace-FOSS is a system for tracking parts along the supply chain. A high level of transparency across the supplier network enables faster intervention based on a recorded event in the supply chain. This saves costs by seamlessly tracking parts and creates trust through clearly defined and secure data access by the companies and persons involved in the process.
More information: https://openapi-generator.tech
Contact Info: team@openapitools.org
Version: 1.0.0
BasePath:/api
License: Apache 2.0
http://apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0.html

Access

  1. OAuth AuthorizationUrl:TokenUrl:localhost

post /alerts
Start alert by part ids (alertAssets)
The endpoint starts alert based on part ids provided.

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

StartQualityNotificationRequest StartQualityNotificationRequest (required)
Body Parameter —

Return type

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

200

Returns the asset by childId

429

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

415

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

403

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

401

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

404

Not found. ErrorResponse
Up 
get /assets/as-built/{assetId}
Get asset by id (assetById1)
The endpoint returns an asset filtered by id .

Path parameters

assetId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null

Return type

array[getDetailInformation_200_response_inner_inner]

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

429

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

415

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

403

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

401

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

200

Returns the assets found

404

Not found. ErrorResponse
Up 
get /assets/as-built
Get assets by pagination (assets)
The endpoint returns a paged result of assets.

Query parameters

pageable (required)
Query Parameter — default: null
searchCriteriaRequestParam (required)
Query Parameter — default: null

Return type

array[array[getDetailInformation_200_response_inner_inner]]

Up 
post /assets/as-built/sync
Synchronizes assets from IRS (sync1)
The endpoint synchronizes the assets from irs.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

SyncAssetsRequest SyncAssetsRequest (required)
Body Parameter —

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

429

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

200

Returns the updated asset

415

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

403

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

401

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

404

Not found. ErrorResponse

AssetsAsPlanned

Up 
get /assets/as-planned/*/children/{childId}
Get asset by child id (assetByChildIdAndAssetId)
The endpoint returns an asset filtered by child id.

Path parameters

childId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null

Return type

array[getDetailInformation_200_response_inner_inner]

Up 
post /assets/as-planned/detail-information
Searches for assets by ids. (getDetailInformation)
The endpoint searchs for assets by id and returns a list of them.

Responses

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

404

Not found. ErrorResponse
Up 
post /assets/as-planned/sync
Synchronizes assets from IRS (sync)
The endpoint synchronizes the assets from irs.

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

SyncAssetsRequest SyncAssetsRequest (required)
Body Parameter —

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

429

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

415

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

403

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

401

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

201

Created.

404

Not found. ErrorResponse
Up 
patch /assets/as-planned/{assetId}
Updates asset (updateAsset)
The endpoint updates asset by provided quality type.

Path parameters

assetId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null

Consumes

This API call consumes the following media types via the Content-Type request header:
  • application/json

Request body

UpdateAssetRequest UpdateAssetRequest (required)
Body Parameter —

Return type

array[getDetailInformation_200_response_inner_inner]

Dashboard

Up 
get /dashboard
Returns dashboard related data (dashboard)
The endpoint can return limited data based on the user role

Return type

DashboardResponse

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "asPlannedSupplierParts" : 3,
  "supplierPartsWithOpenInvestigations" : 2,
  "sentActiveAlerts" : 2,
  "receivedActiveInvestigations" : 2,
  "asPlannedCustomerParts" : 10,
  "asBuiltCustomerParts" : 5,
  "asPlannedOwnParts" : 1,
  "receivedActiveAlerts" : 2,
  "asBuiltSupplierParts" : 2,
  "asBuiltOwnParts" : 1,
  "myPartsWithOpenInvestigations" : 1,
  "sentActiveInvestigations" : 2,
  "myPartsWithOpenAlerts" : 1,
  "supplierPartsWithOpenAlerts" : 1,
  "customerPartsWithOpenAlerts" : 1,
  "customerPartsWithOpenInvestigations" : 2
}

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

429

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

415

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

403

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

401

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

200

Returns dashboard data DashboardResponse

404

Not found. ErrorResponse

ImportReport

Up 
get /assets/import/report/{importJobId}
report of the imported assets (importReport)
This endpoint returns information about the imported assets to Trace-X.

Path parameters

importJobId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null

Return type

ImportReportResponse

Example data

Content-Type: application/json
{
  "importedAsset" : [ {
    "catenaxId" : "urn:uuid:7eeeac86-7b69-444d-81e6-655d0f1513bd}",
    "importedOn" : "2099-02-21T21:27:10.734950Z",
    "importState" : "TRANSIENT",
    "importMessage" : "Asset created successfully in transient state."
  }, {
    "catenaxId" : "urn:uuid:7eeeac86-7b69-444d-81e6-655d0f1513bd}",
    "importedOn" : "2099-02-21T21:27:10.734950Z",
    "importState" : "TRANSIENT",
    "importMessage" : "Asset created successfully in transient state."
  } ],
  "importJob" : {
    "importId" : "456a952e-05eb-40dc-a6f2-9c2cb9c1387f",
    "completedOn" : "2099-02-21T21:27:10.734950Z",
    "startedOn" : "2099-02-21T21:27:10.734950Z",
    "importJobStatus" : "INITIALIZING"
  }
}

  • application/json

OK. ImportReportResponse

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

Investigations

Up 
post /investigations/{investigationId}/approve
Approves investigations by id (approveInvestigation)
The endpoint approves investigations by their id.

Path parameters

investigationId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null format: int64

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

200

Ok.

No content.

Up 
post /investigations/{investigationId}/cancel
Cancles investigations by id (cancelInvestigation)
The endpoint cancles investigations by their id.

Path parameters

investigationId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null format: int64

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.

get /investigations/distinctFilterValues
getDistinctFilterValues (distinctFilterValues)

Produces

This API call produces the following media types according to the Accept request header; the media type will be conveyed by the Content-Type response header.
  • application/json

Responses

429

Too many requests. ErrorResponse

400

Bad request. ErrorResponse

415

Unsupported media type ErrorResponse

500

Internal server error. ErrorResponse

403

Forbidden. ErrorResponse

401

Authorization failed. ErrorResponse

404

Not found. ErrorResponse

200

Returns the paged result found for Asset
Up 
get /investigations/{investigationId}
Gets investigations by id (getInvestigation)
The endpoint returns investigations as paged result by their id.

Path parameters

investigationId (required)
Path Parameter — default: null format: int64

Return type

array[InvestigationResponse]
